* <span data-ttu-id="84764-564">Windows Server 2008 R2 ou version ultérieure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-564">Windows Server 2008 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-565">Le [serveur HTTP.sys](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (anciennement WebListener) ne fonctionne pas dans une configuration de proxy inverse avec IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-565">[HTTP.sys server](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (formerly called WebListener) doesn't work in a reverse proxy configuration with IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-566">Utilisez le [serveur Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-566">Use the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-567">Pour plus d’informations sur l’hébergement dans Azure, consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-567">For information on hosting in Azure, see <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-568">Pour obtenir des conseils de dépannage, consultez <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-568">For troubleshooting guidance, see <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-569">Plateformes prises en charge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-569">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-570">Les applications publiées pour les déploiements 32 bits (x86) ou 64 bits (x64) sont prises en charge.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-570">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-571">Déployez une application 32 bits avec un kit SDK .NET Core (x86) de 32 bits, sauf si l’application :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-571">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="84764-572">Nécessite l’espace d’adressage de mémoire virtuelle le plus grand disponible pour une application 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-572">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="84764-573">Nécessite la taille de pile IIS la plus grande disponible.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-573">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="84764-574">A des dépendances natives 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-574">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-575">Utilisez un kit SDK .NET Core 64 bits (x64) pour publier une application 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-575">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-576">Un runtime 64 bits doit être présent sur le système hôte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-576">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

## <a name="hosting-models"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-577">Modèles d'hébergement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-577">Hosting models</span></span>

### <a name="in-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-578">Modèle d’hébergement in-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-578">In-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-579">En utilisant l’hébergement in-process, une application ASP.NET Core s’exécute dans le même processus que son processus de travail IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-579">Using in-process hosting, an ASP.NET Core app runs in the same process as its IIS worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-580">L’hébergement in-process offre des performances améliorées par rapport à l’hébergement out-of-process, car :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-580">In-process hosting provides improved performance over out-of-process hosting because:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="84764-581">Les requêtes ne sont pas transmises par proxy sur la carte de bouclage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-581">Requests aren't proxied over the loopback adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-582">Une carte de bouclage est une interface réseau qui renvoie le trafic réseau sortant vers le même ordinateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-582">A loopback adapter is a network interface that returns outgoing network traffic back to the same machine.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-583">IIS s’occupe de la gestion des processus par l’intermédiaire du [service d’activation des processus Windows (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-583">IIS handles process management with the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-584">[Module ASP.net Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-584">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module):</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="84764-585">Effectue l’initialisation de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-585">Performs app initialization.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="84764-586">Charge le [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-586">Loads the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr).</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="84764-587">Appelle `Program.Main`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-587">Calls `Program.Main`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="84764-588">Gère la durée de vie de la requête native IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-588">Handles the lifetime of the IIS native request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-589">Le modèle d’hébergement in-process n’est pas pris en charge pour les applications ASP.NET Core qui ciblent le .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-589">The in-process hosting model isn't supported for ASP.NET Core apps that target the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-590">Le schéma suivant montre la relation entre IIS, le module ASP.NET Core et une application hébergée dans un processus :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-590">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted in-process:</span></span>

![Module ASP.NET Core dans le scénario d’hébergement in-process](index/_static/ancm-inprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="84764-592">Une requête arrive du web au pilote HTTP.sys en mode noyau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-592">A request arrives from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-593">Le pilote achemine la requête native vers IIS sur le port configuré du site web, généralement 80 (HTTP) ou 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-593">The driver routes the native request to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-594">Le module ASP.NET Core reçoit la demande native et la transmet au serveur HTTP IIS ( `IISHttpServer` ).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-594">The ASP.NET Core Module receives the native request and passes it to IIS HTTP Server (`IISHttpServer`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-595">Le serveur HTTP IIS est une implémentation du serveur in-process pour IIS qui convertit la requête native en requête managée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-595">IIS HTTP Server is an in-process server implementation for IIS that converts the request from native to managed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-596">Une fois que IIS HTTP Server a traité la requête, celle-ci est envoyée (push) dans le pipeline de middleware (intergiciel) d’ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-596">After the IIS HTTP Server processes the request, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-597">Le pipeline de middlewares traite la requête et la passe en tant qu’instance de `HttpContext` à la logique de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-597">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-598">La réponse de l’application est retransmise à IIS via le serveur HTTP IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-598">The app's response is passed back to IIS through IIS HTTP Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-599">IIS envoie la réponse au client qui a initié la demande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-599">IIS sends the response to the client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-600">L’hébergement in-process est au choix pour les applications existantes, mais les modèles [dotnet new](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-new) sont définis par défaut sur le modèle d’hébergement in-process pour tous les scénarios IIS et IIS Express.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-600">In-process hosting is opt-in for existing apps, but [dotnet new](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-new) templates default to the in-process hosting model for all IIS and IIS Express scenarios.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-601">`CreateDefaultBuilder` appelle une instance <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer> en appelant la méthode <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS*> pour démarrer [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) et héberger l’application dans le processus Worker IIS (*w3wp.exe* ou *iisexpress.exe*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-601">`CreateDefaultBuilder` adds an <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer> instance by calling the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS*> method to boot the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) and host the app inside of the IIS worker process (*w3wp.exe* or *iisexpress.exe*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-602">Les tests de performance indiquent que l’hébergement d’une application.NET Core in-process fournit un débit de requêtes beaucoup plus élevé que l’hébergement de l’application out-of-process et la redirection par le biais d’un proxy des requêtes vers le serveur [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-602">Performance tests indicate that hosting a .NET Core app in-process delivers significantly higher request throughput compared to hosting the app out-of-process and proxying requests to [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) server.</span></span>

### <a name="out-of-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-603">Modèle d’hébergement out-of-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-603">Out-of-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-604">Étant donné que ASP.NET Core applications s’exécutent dans un processus distinct du processus de travail IIS, le module ASP.NET Core gère la gestion des processus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-604">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the ASP.NET Core Module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-605">Le module démarre le processus pour l’application ASP.NET Core quand la première requête arrive, et il redémarre l’application si elle s’arrête ou se bloque.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-605">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-606">Il s’agit essentiellement du même comportement que celui des applications s’exécutant in-process, et qui sont gérées par le [service d’activation des processus Windows (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-606">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-607">Le schéma suivant illustre la relation entre IIS, le module ASP.NET Core et une application hébergée hors processus :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-607">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![Module ASP.NET Core dans le scénario d’hébergement out-of-process](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="84764-609">Les requêtes arrivent du web au pilote HTTP.sys en mode noyau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-609">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-610">Le pilote route les requêtes vers IIS sur le port configuré du site web, généralement 80 (HTTP) ou 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-610">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-611">Le module transfère les requêtes à Kestrel sur un port aléatoire pour l’application, qui n’est ni le port 80 ni le port 443.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-611">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app, which isn't port 80 or 443.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-612">Le module spécifie le port via une variable d’environnement au démarrage, et l’extension <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> configure le serveur pour qu’il écoute sur `http://localhost:{PORT}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-612">The module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup, and the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> extension configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{PORT}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-613">Des vérifications supplémentaires sont effectuées, et les requêtes qui ne proviennent pas du module sont rejetées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-613">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-614">Le module ne prend pas en charge le transfert HTTPS : les requêtes sont donc transférées via HTTP, même si IIS les reçoit via HTTPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-614">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding, so requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-615">Dès que Kestrel sélectionne la requête dans le module, celle-ci est envoyée (push) dans le pipeline de middlewares d’ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-615">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-616">Le pipeline de middlewares traite la requête et la passe en tant qu’instance de `HttpContext` à la logique de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-616">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-617">L’intergiciel (middleware) ajouté par l’intégration d’IIS met à jour le schéma, l’adresse IP distante et la base du chemin pour prendre en compte le transfert de la requête à Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-617">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-618">La réponse de l’application est ensuite repassée à IIS, qui la renvoie au client HTTP à l’origine de la requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-618">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which pushes it back out to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-619">Pour obtenir de l’aide sur la configuration du module ASP.NET Core, consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-619">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-620">Pour plus d’informations sur l’hébergement, consultez [Héberger dans ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-620">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-621">Configuration de l’application</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-621">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-622">Activer les composants IISIntegration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-622">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-623">Lors de la création d’un ordinateur hôte dans `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), appelez <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder*> pour activer l’intégration d’IIS :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-623">When building a host in `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder*> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IWebHostBuilder CreateWebHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```

<span data-ttu-id="84764-624">Pour plus d'informations sur le `CreateDefaultBuilder`, consultez <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-624">For more information on `CreateDefaultBuilder`, see <xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#set-up-a-host>.</span></span>

### <a name="iis-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-625">Options IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-625">IIS options</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-626">**Modèle d’hébergement in-process**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-626">**In-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-627">Pour configurer les options IIS Server, incluez une configuration de service pour <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> dans <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-627">To configure IIS Server options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-628">L’exemple suivant désactive AutomaticAuthentication :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-628">The following example disables AutomaticAuthentication:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISServerOptions>(options => 
{
    options.AutomaticAuthentication = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="84764-629">Option</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-629">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="84764-630">Default</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-630">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="84764-631">Paramètre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-631">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="84764-632">Si `true`, IIS Server définit le `HttpContext.User` authentifié par [Authentification Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-632">If `true`, IIS Server sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-633">Si `false`, le serveur fournit uniquement une identité pour `HttpContext.User` et répond aux questions explicitement posées par `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-633">If `false`, the server only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-634">L’authentification Windows doit être activée dans IIS pour que `AutomaticAuthentication` fonctionne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-634">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-635">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [authentification Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-635">For more information, see [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="84764-636">Définit le nom d’affichage montré aux utilisateurs sur les pages de connexion.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-636">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="84764-637">**Modèle d’hébergement out-of-process**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-637">**Out-of-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-638">Pour configurer les options IIS, incluez une configuration de service pour <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> dans <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-638">To configure IIS options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-639">L’exemple suivant empêche l’application d’être renseignée `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-639">The following example prevents the app from populating `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISOptions>(options => 
{
    options.ForwardClientCertificate = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="84764-640">Option</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-640">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="84764-641">Default</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-641">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="84764-642">Paramètre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-642">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="84764-643">Si la valeur est `true`, le [middleware d’intégration IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) définit l’élément `HttpContext.User` authentifié par [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-643">If `true`, [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-644">Si `false`, l’intergiciel (middleware) fournit uniquement une identité pour `HttpContext.User` et répond aux questions explicitement posées par `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-644">If `false`, the middleware only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-645">L’authentification Windows doit être activée dans IIS pour que `AutomaticAuthentication` fonctionne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-645">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-646">Pour plus d'informations, consultez la rubrique [Authentification Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-646">For more information, see the [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth) topic.</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="84764-647">Définit le nom d’affichage montré aux utilisateurs sur les pages de connexion.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-647">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `ForwardClientCertificate`     | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="84764-648">Si la valeur est `true` et que l’en-tête de requête `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` est présent, `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` est renseigné.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-648">If `true` and the `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` request header is present, the `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` is populated.</span></span> |

### <a name="proxy-server-and-load-balancer-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-649">Scénarios avec un serveur proxy et un équilibreur de charge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-649">Proxy server and load balancer scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-650">Le [middleware d’intégration IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), qui configure le middleware des en-têtes transférés, et le module ASP.NET Core sont configurés pour transférer le schéma (HTTP/HTTPS) et l’adresse IP distante d’où provient la requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-650">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), which configures Forwarded Headers Middleware, and the ASP.NET Core Module are configured to forward the scheme (HTTP/HTTPS) and the remote IP address where the request originated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-651">Une configuration supplémentaire peut être nécessaire pour les applications hébergées derrière des serveurs proxy et des équilibreurs de charge supplémentaires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-651">Additional configuration might be required for apps hosted behind additional proxy servers and load balancers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-652">Pour plus d’informations, consultez l’article [Configurer ASP.NET Core pour l’utilisation de serveurs proxy et d’équilibreurs de charge](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-652">For more information, see [Configure ASP.NET Core to work with proxy servers and load balancers](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-653">fichier web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-653">web.config file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-654">Le fichier *web.config* configure le [Module ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-654">The *web.config* file configures the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-655">La création, la transformation et la publication du fichier *web.config* sont gérées par une cible MSBuild (`_TransformWebConfig`) quand le projet est publié.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-655">Creating, transforming, and publishing the *web.config* file is handled by an MSBuild target (`_TransformWebConfig`) when the project is published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-656">Cette cible est présente dans les cibles du SDK web (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-656">This target is present in the Web SDK targets (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-657">Le SDK est défini en haut du fichier projet :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-657">The SDK is set at the top of the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web">
```

<span data-ttu-id="84764-658">Si le projet ne contient pas de fichier *web.config*, le fichier est créé avec le *processPath* et les *arguments* corrects pour configurer le Module ASP.NET Core, puis il est déplacé vers la [sortie publiée](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-658">If a *web.config* file isn't present in the project, the file is created with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to [published output](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-659">Si un fichier *web.config* se trouve dans le projet, il est transformé avec le *processPath* et les *arguments* corrects pour configurer le Module ASP.NET Core, puis il est déplacé vers la sortie publiée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-659">If a *web.config* file is present in the project, the file is transformed with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to published output.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-660">La transformation ne modifie pas les paramètres de configuration IIS dans le fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-660">The transformation doesn't modify IIS configuration settings in the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-661">Le fichier *web.config* peut fournir des paramètres de configuration IIS supplémentaires qui contrôlent les modules IIS actifs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-661">The *web.config* file may provide additional IIS configuration settings that control active IIS modules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-662">Pour plus d’informations sur les modules IIS capables de traiter les requêtes avec des applications ASP.NET Core, consultez la rubrique [Modules IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-662">For information on IIS modules that are capable of processing requests with ASP.NET Core apps, see the [IIS modules](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules) topic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-663">Pour empêcher le kit de développement logiciel (SDK) Web de transformer le fichier *web.config* , utilisez la **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** propriété dans le fichier projet :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-663">To prevent the Web SDK from transforming the *web.config* file, use the **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** property in the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<PropertyGroup>
  <IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>true</IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>
</PropertyGroup>
```

<span data-ttu-id="84764-664">Lorsque vous désactivez le Kit de développement logiciel (SDK) Web en transformant le fichier, le *processPath* et les *arguments* doivent être définis manuellement par le développeur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-664">When disabling the Web SDK from transforming the file, the *processPath* and *arguments* should be manually set by the developer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-665">Pour plus d'informations, consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-665">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file-location"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-666">emplacement du fichier web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-666">web.config file location</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-667">Pour configurer correctement le [Module ASP.net Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) , le fichier *web.config* doit être présent au chemin d’accès [racine du contenu](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) (en général, le chemin d’accès de base de l’application) de l’application déployée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-667">In order to set up the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) correctly, the *web.config* file must be present at the [content root](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) path (typically the app base path) of the deployed app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-668">Il s’agit du même emplacement que le chemin physique du site Web fourni à IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-668">This is the same location as the website physical path provided to IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-669">Le fichier *web.config* est nécessaire à la racine de l’application pour permettre la publication de plusieurs applications à l’aide de Web Deploy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-669">The *web.config* file is required at the root of the app to enable the publishing of multiple apps using Web Deploy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-670">Des fichiers sensibles existent sur le chemin d’accès physique de l’application, par exemple \* \<assembly>.runtimeconfig.jssur*, \* \<assembly> . xml* (commentaires de documentation XML) et \* \<assembly>.deps.jssur\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-670">Sensitive files exist on the app's physical path, such as *\<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*, *\<assembly>.xml* (XML Documentation comments), and *\<assembly>.deps.json*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-671">Lorsque le fichier *web.config* est présent et que le site démarre normalement, IIS ne traite pas ces fichiers sensibles s’ils sont demandés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-671">When the *web.config* file is present and the site starts normally, IIS doesn't serve these sensitive files if they're requested.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-672">Si le fichier *web.config* est absent, nommé de manière incorrecte ou s’il est incapable de configurer le site pour un démarrage normal, IIS peut traiter des fichiers sensibles publiquement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-672">If the *web.config* file is missing, incorrectly named, or unable to configure the site for normal startup, IIS may serve sensitive files publicly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-673">**Le fichier *web.config* doit être présent dans le déploiement à tout moment, correctement nommé et capable de configurer le site pour un démarrage normal. Ne supprimez jamais le fichier *web.config* d’un déploiement de production.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-673">**The *web.config* file must be present in the deployment at all times, correctly named, and able to configure the site for normal start up. Never remove the *web.config* file from a production deployment.**</span></span>

### <a name="transform-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-674">Transformer web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-674">Transform web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-675">Si vous devez transformer *web.config* lors de la publication (par exemple, définir les variables d’environnement basées sur la configuration, le profil ou l’environnement), consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-675">If you need to transform *web.config* on publish (for example, set environment variables based on the configuration, profile, or environment), see <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span></span>

## <a name="iis-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-676">Configuration d’IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-676">IIS configuration</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-677">**Systèmes d’exploitation Windows Server**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-677">**Windows Server operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-678">Activez le rôle serveur **Serveur Web (IIS)** et établissez des services de rôle.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-678">Enable the **Web Server (IIS)** server role and establish role services.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-679">Utilisez l’Assistant **Ajouter des rôles et des fonctionnalités** par le biais du menu **Gérer** ou du lien dans **Gestionnaire de serveur**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-679">Use the **Add Roles and Features** wizard from the **Manage** menu or the link in **Server Manager**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-680">À l’étape **Rôles de serveurs**, cochez la case **Serveur Web (IIS)**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-680">On the **Server Roles** step, check the box for **Web Server (IIS)**.</span></span>

   ![Le rôle Serveur Web IIS est sélectionné à l’étape Sélectionner des rôles de serveurs.](index/_static/server-roles-ws2016.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-682">Après l’étape **Fonctionnalités**, l’étape **Services de rôle** se charge pour le serveur Web (IIS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-682">After the **Features** step, the **Role services** step loads for Web Server (IIS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-683">Sélectionnez les services de rôle IIS souhaités ou acceptez les services de rôle par défaut fournis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-683">Select the IIS role services desired or accept the default role services provided.</span></span>

   ![Les services de rôle par défaut sont sélectionnés à l’étape Sélectionner des services de rôle.](index/_static/role-services-ws2016.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="84764-685">**Authentification Windows (facultatif)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-685">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="84764-686">Pour activer l’authentification Windows, développez les nœuds suivants : sécurité du **serveur Web**  >  **Security**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-686">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-687">Sélectionnez la fonctionnalité **Authentification Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-687">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-688">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [authentification \<windowsAuthentication> Windows](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) et [configurer l’authentification Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-688">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="84764-689">**WebSockets (facultatif)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-689">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="84764-690">WebSockets est pris en charge avec ASP.NET Core 1.1 ou version ultérieure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-690">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-691">Pour activer les WebSockets, développez les nœuds suivants : développement d’applications de **serveur Web**  >  **Application Development**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-691">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Application Development**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-692">Sélectionnez la fonctionnalité **Protocole WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-692">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-693">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-693">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-694">Validez l’étape de **Confirmation** pour installer les services et le rôle de serveur web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-694">Proceed through the **Confirmation** step to install the web server role and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-695">Un redémarrage du serveur/d’IIS n’est pas nécessaire après l’installation du rôle **Serveur Web (IIS)**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-695">A server/IIS restart isn't required after installing the **Web Server (IIS)** role.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-696">**Systèmes d’exploitation Windows Desktop**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-696">**Windows desktop operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-697">Activez la **Console de gestion IIS** et les **Services World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-697">Enable the **IIS Management Console** and **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-698">Naviguez jusqu’à **Panneau de configuration** > **Programmes** > **Programmes et fonctionnalités** > **Activer ou désactiver des fonctionnalités Windows** (à gauche de l’écran).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-698">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-699">Ouvrez le nœud **Internet Information Services**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-699">Open the **Internet Information Services** node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-700">Ouvrez le nœud **Outils de gestion Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-700">Open the **Web Management Tools** node.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-701">Cochez la case **Console de gestion IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-701">Check the box for **IIS Management Console**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-702">Cochez la case **Services World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-702">Check the box for **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-703">Acceptez les fonctionnalités par défaut pour **Services World Wide Web** ou personnalisez les fonctionnalités d’IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-703">Accept the default features for **World Wide Web Services** or customize the IIS features.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="84764-704">**Authentification Windows (facultatif)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-704">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="84764-705">Pour activer l’authentification Windows, développez les nœuds suivants : **World Wide webing services**  >  **Security**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-705">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-706">Sélectionnez la fonctionnalité **Authentification Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-706">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-707">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [authentification \<windowsAuthentication> Windows](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) et [configurer l’authentification Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-707">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="84764-708">**WebSockets (facultatif)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-708">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="84764-709">WebSockets est pris en charge avec ASP.NET Core 1.1 ou version ultérieure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-709">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-710">Pour activer WebSockets, développez les nœuds suivants : fonctionnalités de développement d’applications **World Wide Web services**  >  **Application Development Features**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-710">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-711">Sélectionnez la fonctionnalité **Protocole WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-711">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-712">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-712">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-713">Si l’installation d’IIS requiert un redémarrage, redémarrez le système.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-713">If the IIS installation requires a restart, restart the system.</span></span>

## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-715">Installer le bundle d’hébergement .NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-715">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-716">Installez le *bundle d’hébergement .NET Core* sur le système hôte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-716">Install the *.NET Core Hosting Bundle* on the hosting system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-717">L’offre groupée installe le Runtime .NET Core, la bibliothèque .NET Core et le [Module ASP.net Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-717">The bundle installs the .NET Core Runtime, .NET Core Library, and the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-718">Le module permet aux applications ASP.NET Core de s’exécuter derrière IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-718">The module allows ASP.NET Core apps to run behind IIS.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="84764-719">Si le bundle d’hébergement est installé avant IIS, l’installation du bundle doit être réparée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-719">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-720">Après avoir installé IIS, réexécutez le programme d’installation du bundle d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-720">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="84764-721">Si le bundle d’hébergement est installé après l’installation de la version 64 bits (x 64) de .NET Core, les SDK peuvent apparaître manquants ([Aucun SDK .NET Core n’a été détecté](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-721">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-722">Pour résoudre le problème, consultez <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-722">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

### <a name="download"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-723">Téléchargement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-723">Download</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-724">Accédez à la page [Télécharger .net Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-724">Navigate to the [Download .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) page.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-725">Sélectionnez la version .NET Core de votre choix.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-725">Select the desired .NET Core version.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-726">Dans la colonne **Run apps - Runtime**, recherchez la ligne de la version du runtime .NET Core souhaitée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-726">In the **Run apps - Runtime** column, find the row of the .NET Core runtime version desired.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-727">Téléchargez le programme d’installation à l’aide du lien d' **hébergement** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-727">Download the installer using the **Hosting Bundle** link.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="84764-728">Certains programmes d’installation contiennent des versions qui sont arrivées à leur fin de vie (EOL) et qui ne sont plus prises en charge par Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-728">Some installers contain release versions that have reached their end of life (EOL) and are no longer supported by Microsoft.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-729">Pour plus d’informations, consultez la [politique de support](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-729">For more information, see the [support policy](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span></span>

### <a name="install-the-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-730">Installer le bundle d’hébergement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-730">Install the Hosting Bundle</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-731">Exécutez le programme d’installation sur le serveur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-731">Run the installer on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-732">Les paramètres suivants sont disponibles lorsque vous exécutez le programme d’installation à partir d’un shell de commande administrateur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-732">The following parameters are available when running the installer from an administrator command shell:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="84764-733">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Ignorez l’installation du module ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-733">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="84764-734">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Ignorez l’installation du Runtime .NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-734">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-735">Utilisé lorsque le serveur héberge uniquement [des déploiements autonomes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-735">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="84764-736">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Ignorez l’installation du Framework partagé ASP.NET (runtime ASP.NET).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-736">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-737">Utilisé lorsque le serveur héberge uniquement [des déploiements autonomes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-737">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="84764-738">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Ignorez l’installation des runtimes x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-738">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Skip installing x86 runtimes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-739">Utilisez ce paramètre lorsque vous savez que vous n’hébergerez pas d’applications 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-739">Use this parameter when you know that you won't be hosting 32-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-740">Si vous n’excluez pas d’avoir à héberger des applications 32 bits et 64 bits dans le futur, n'utilisez pas ce paramètre et installez les deux runtimes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-740">If there's any chance that you will host both 32-bit and 64-bit apps in the future, don't use this parameter and install both runtimes.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="84764-741">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Désactive la vérification de l’utilisation d’une configuration partagée IIS lorsque la configuration partagée (*applicationHost.config*) se trouve sur le même ordinateur que l’installation d’IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-741">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Disable the check for using an IIS Shared Configuration when the shared configuration (*applicationHost.config*) is on the same machine as the IIS installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-742">*Disponible uniquement pour les programmes d’installation du pack d’hébergement ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou version ultérieure.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-742">*Only available for ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later Hosting Bundler installers.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-743">Pour plus d'informations, consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-743">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-744">Redémarrez le système ou exécutez les commandes suivantes dans une interface de commande :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-744">Restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

   ```console
   net stop was /y
   net start w3svc
   ```
   <span data-ttu-id="84764-745">Le redémarrage d’IIS récupère une modification apportée au CHEMIN D’ACCÈS du système, qui est une variable d’environnement, par le programme d’installation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-745">Restarting IIS picks up a change to the system PATH, which is an environment variable, made by the installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-746">Il n’est pas nécessaire d’arrêter manuellement des sites individuels dans IIS lors de l’installation du bundle d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-746">It isn't necessary to manually stop individual sites in IIS when installing the Hosting Bundle.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-747">Les applications hébergées (sites IIS) redémarrent lors du redémarrage d’IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-747">Hosted apps (IIS sites) restart when IIS restarts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-748">Les applications redémarrent lorsqu’elles reçoivent leur première requête, y compris à partir du [module d’initialisation](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout)de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-748">Apps start up again when they receive their first request, including from the [Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-749">ASP.NET Core adopte le comportement de restauration par progression pour les mises à jour correctives des packages d’infrastructure partagés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-749">ASP.NET Core adopts roll-forward behavior for patch releases of shared framework packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-750">Lorsque les applications hébergées par IIS redémarrent avec IIS, elles sont chargées avec les dernières versions de correctif de leurs packages référencés lorsqu’elles reçoivent leur première demande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-750">When apps hosted by IIS restart with IIS, the apps load with the latest patch releases of their referenced packages when they receive their first request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-751">Si IIS n’est pas redémarré, les applications redémarrent et présentent le comportement de restauration par progression lorsque leurs processus de travail sont recyclés et qu’ils reçoivent leur première demande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-751">If IIS isn't restarted, apps restart and exhibit roll-forward behavior when their worker processes are recycled and they receive their first request.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="84764-752">Pour plus d’informations sur la configuration partagée IIS, consultez [Module ASP.NET Core avec configuration partagée des services Internet (IIS)](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-752">For information on IIS Shared Configuration, see [ASP.NET Core Module with IIS Shared Configuration](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span></span>

## <a name="install-web-deploy-when-publishing-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-753">Installer Web Deploy lors de la publication avec Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-753">Install Web Deploy when publishing with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-754">Quand vous déployez des applications sur un serveur avec [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), installez la dernière version de Web Deploy sur le serveur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-754">When deploying apps to servers with [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), install the latest version of Web Deploy on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-755">Pour installer Web Deploy, utilisez [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) ou obtenez un programme d’installation directement à partir du [Centre de téléchargement Microsoft](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-755">To install Web Deploy, use the [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) or obtain an installer directly from the [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-756">La méthode recommandée est d’utiliser WebPI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-756">The preferred method is to use WebPI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-757">WebPI offre une installation autonome et une configuration pour les fournisseurs d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-757">WebPI offers a standalone setup and a configuration for hosting providers.</span></span>

## <a name="create-the-iis-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-758">Créer le site IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-758">Create the IIS site</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-759">Sur le système d’hébergement, créez un dossier pour contenir les fichiers et dossiers publiés de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-759">On the hosting system, create a folder to contain the app's published folders and files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-760">À l’étape suivante, le chemin du dossier est fourni à IIS en tant que chemin d’accès physique à l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-760">In a following step, the folder's path is provided to IIS as the physical path to the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-761">Pour plus d’informations sur le dossier de déploiement et la disposition d’un fichier d’une application, consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-761">For more information on an app's deployment folder and file layout, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-762">Dans le gestionnaire des services Internet, ouvrez le nœud du serveur dans le panneau **connexions** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-762">In IIS Manager, open the server's node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-763">Cliquez avec le bouton de droite sur le dossier **Sites**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-763">Right-click the **Sites** folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-764">Sélectionnez **Ajouter un site Web** dans le menu contextuel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-764">Select **Add Website** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-765">Spécifiez le **Nom du site** et définissez le **Chemin physique** sur le dossier de déploiement de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-765">Provide a **Site name** and set the **Physical path** to the app's deployment folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-766">Fournissez la configuration de **liaison** et créez le site Web en sélectionnant **OK**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-766">Provide the **Binding** configuration and create the website by selecting **OK**:</span></span>

   ![Spécifiez le nom du site, le chemin physique et le nom d’hôte à l’étape Ajouter un site Web.](index/_static/add-website-ws2016.png)

   > [!WARNING]
   > <span data-ttu-id="84764-768">Les liaisons génériques de niveau supérieur (`http://*:80/` et `http://+:80`) ne doivent **pas** être utilisées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-768">Top-level wildcard bindings (`http://*:80/` and `http://+:80`) should **not** be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-769">Les liaisons génériques de niveau supérieur peuvent exposer votre application à des failles de sécurité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-769">Top-level wildcard bindings can open up your app to security vulnerabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-770">Cela s’applique aux caractères génériques forts et faibles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-770">This applies to both strong and weak wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-771">Utilisez des noms d’hôte explicites plutôt que des caractères génériques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-771">Use explicit host names rather than wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-772">Une liaison générique de sous-domaine (par exemple, `*.mysub.com`) ne présente pas ce risque de sécurité si vous contrôlez le domaine parent en entier (par opposition à `*.com`, qui est vulnérable).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-772">Subdomain wildcard binding (for example, `*.mysub.com`) doesn't have this security risk if you control the entire parent domain (as opposed to `*.com`, which is vulnerable).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-773">Consultez la [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) pour plus d’informations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-773">See [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) for more information.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-774">Sous le nœud du serveur, sélectionnez **Pools d’applications**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-774">Under the server's node, select **Application Pools**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-775">Cliquez avec le bouton de droite sur le pool d’applications du site et sélectionnez **Paramètres de base** dans le menu contextuel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-775">Right-click the site's app pool and select **Basic Settings** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-776">Dans la fenêtre **Modifier le pool d’applications**, définissez la **version .NET CLR** sur **Aucun code managé** :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-776">In the **Edit Application Pool** window, set the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code**:</span></span>

   ![Définissez Aucun code managé pour la version CLR .NET.](index/_static/edit-apppool-ws2016.png)

    <span data-ttu-id="84764-778">ASP.NET Core s’exécute dans un processus séparé et gère l’exécution.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-778">ASP.NET Core runs in a separate process and manages the runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-779">ASP.NET Core ne repose pas sur le chargement de Desktop CLR (CLR .NET)&mdash;la prise en charge du Common Language Runtime Core (CoreCLR) pour .NET Core est démarrée pour héberger l’application dans le processus Worker.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-779">ASP.NET Core doesn't rely on loading the desktop CLR (.NET CLR)&mdash;the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-780">La configuration de la **version CLR .NET** sur **Aucun code managé** est facultative, mais recommandée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-780">Setting the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** is optional but recommended.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-781">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou version ultérieure* : pour un [déploiement autonome](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) 64 bits (x64) qui utilise le [modèle d’hébergement In-process](#in-process-hosting-model), désactivez le pool d’applications pour les processus 32 bits (x86).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-781">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later*: For a 64-bit (x64) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), disable the app pool for 32-bit (x86) processes.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="84764-782">Dans la barre latérale **Actions** du gestionnaire IIS > **Pools d’applications**, sélectionnez **Définir les valeurs par défaut du pool d’applications** ou **Paramètres avancés**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-782">In the **Actions** sidebar of IIS Manager > **Application Pools**, select **Set Application Pool Defaults** or **Advanced Settings**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-783">Recherchez **Activer les applications 32 bits** et définissez la valeur sur `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-783">Locate **Enable 32-Bit Applications** and set the value to `False`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-784">Ce paramètre n’affecte pas les applications déployées pour l’[hébergement Out-of-process](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-784">This setting doesn't affect apps deployed for [out-of-process hosting](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="84764-785">Vérifiez que l’identité de modèle de processus dispose des autorisations appropriées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-785">Confirm the process model identity has the proper permissions.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="84764-786">Si l’identité par défaut du pool d’applications (**modèle de processus**  >  **Identity** ) est \*\* Identity \*\* remplacée par une autre identité, vérifiez que la nouvelle identité dispose des autorisations nécessaires pour accéder au dossier de l’application, à la base de données et à d’autres ressources requises.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-786">If the default identity of the app pool (**Process Model** > **Identity**) is changed from **ApplicationPoolIdentity** to another identity, verify that the new identity has the required permissions to access the app's folder, database, and other required resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-787">Par exemple, le pool d’applications nécessite l’accès en lecture et en écriture aux dossiers dans lesquels l’application lit et écrit des fichiers.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-787">For example, the app pool requires read and write access to folders where the app reads and writes files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-788">**Configuration de l’authentification Windows (facultatif)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-788">**Windows Authentication configuration (Optional)**</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="84764-789">Pour plus d'informations, consultez la rubrique [Configurer l’authentification Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-789">For more information, see [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="deploy-the-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-790">Déployer l’application</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-790">Deploy the app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-791">Déployez l’application dans le dossier **Chemin d’accès physique** IIS qui a été créé dans la section [Créer le site IIS](#create-the-iis-site).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-791">Deploy the app to the IIS **Physical path** folder that was established in the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-792">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) est le mécanisme recommandé pour le déploiement, mais il existe plusieurs options pour déplacer l’application à partir du dossier *publier* du projet vers le dossier de déploiement du système d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-792">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) is the recommended mechanism for deployment, but several options exist for moving the app from the project's *publish* folder to the hosting system's deployment folder.</span></span>

### <a name="web-deploy-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-793">Web Deploy avec Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-793">Web Deploy with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-794">Pour découvrir comment créer un profil de publication pour une utilisation avec Web Deploy, consultez la rubrique [Profils de publication Visual Studio pour le déploiement d’applications ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-794">See the [Visual Studio publish profiles for ASP.NET Core app deployment](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) topic to learn how to create a publish profile for use with Web Deploy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-795">Si le fournisseur d’hébergement fournit un profil de publication ou prend en charge sa création, téléchargez son profil et importez-le à l’aide de la boîte de dialogue **Publier** de Visual Studio :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-795">If the hosting provider provides a Publish Profile or support for creating one, download their profile and import it using the Visual Studio **Publish** dialog:</span></span>

![Boîte de dialogue Publier](index/_static/pub-dialog.png)

### <a name="web-deploy-outside-of-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-797">Web Deploy en dehors de Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-797">Web Deploy outside of Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-798">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) peut également être utilisé en dehors de Visual Studio à partir de la ligne de commande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-798">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) can also be used outside of Visual Studio from the command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-799">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [Web Deployment Tool (Outil de déploiement Web)](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-799">For more information, see [Web Deployment Tool](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span></span>

### <a name="alternatives-to-web-deploy"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-800">Alternatives à Web Deploy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-800">Alternatives to Web Deploy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-801">Utilisez la méthode de votre choix, telle que la copie manuelle, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy) ou [PowerShell](/powershell/), pour déplacer l’application vers le système d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-801">Use any of several methods to move the app to the hosting system, such as manual copy, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy), or [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-802">Pour plus d’informations sur le déploiement d’ASP.NET Core sur IIS, consultez la section [Déploiement de ressources pour les administrateurs IIS](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-802">For more information on ASP.NET Core deployment to IIS, see the [Deployment resources for IIS administrators](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators) section.</span></span>

## <a name="browse-the-website"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-803">Parcourir le site Web</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-803">Browse the website</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-804">Une fois que l’application est déployée sur le système hôte, envoyez une requête à l’un des points de terminaison publics de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-804">After the app is deployed to the hosting system, make a request to one of the app's public endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-805">Dans l’exemple suivant, le site est lié à un **nom d’hôte** IIS de `www.mysite.com` sur le **Port** `80`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-805">In the following example, the site is bound to an IIS **Host name** of `www.mysite.com` on **Port** `80`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-806">Une demande est faite à `http://www.mysite.com` :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-806">A request is made to `http://www.mysite.com`:</span></span>

![Le navigateur Microsoft Edge a chargé la page de démarrage IIS.](index/_static/browsewebsite.png)

## <a name="locked-deployment-files"></a><span data-ttu-id="84764-808">Fichiers de déploiement verrouillés</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-808">Locked deployment files</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="84764-809">Les fichiers dans le dossier de déploiement sont verrouillés quand l’application est en cours d’exécution.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-809">Files in the deployment folder are locked when the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-810">Les fichiers verrouillés ne peuvent pas être remplacés au cours du déploiement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-810">Locked files can't be overwritten during deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-811">Pour libérer des fichiers verrouillés dans un déploiement, arrêtez le pool d’applications à l’aide **d’une** des approches suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-811">To release locked files in a deployment, stop the app pool using **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="84764-812">Utilisez Web Deploy et référencez `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` dans le fichier projet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-812">Use Web Deploy and reference `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` in the project file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-813">Un fichier *app_offline.htm* est placé à la racine du répertoire de l’application web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-813">An *app_offline.htm* file is placed at the root of the web app directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-814">Quand le fichier est présent, le module ASP.NET Core ferme l’application normalement et sert le fichier *app_offline.htm* pendant le déploiement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-814">When the file is present, the ASP.NET Core Module gracefully shuts down the app and serves the *app_offline.htm* file during the deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="84764-815">Pour plus d’informations, consultez les [Informations de référence sur la configuration du module ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-815">For more information, see the [ASP.NET Core Module configuration reference](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="84764-816">Arrêtez manuellement le pool d’applications dans le Gestionnaire IIS sur le serveur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="84764-816">Manually stop the app pool in the IIS Manager on the server.</span></span>
